href=\"https://politicaldig.com/republicans-are-trying-to-block-newly-registered-voters-from-runoff-election-in-georgia/#respond\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li class=\"mvp-post-soc-com mvp-com-click\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<i class=\"fa fa-2 fa-commenting\" aria-hidden=\"true\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</ul>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div><!--mvp-post-soc-wrap-->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"mvp-post-soc-in\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div id=\"mvp-content-main\" class=\"left relative\" itemprop=\"articleBody\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Five civil rights and civic engagement groups have filed suit against Georgia and its secretary of state, Brian Kemp (R), for attempting to block registered voters from participating in a closely watched <a href=\"http://politicaldig.com/trump-fires-off-a-delusional-tweet-declaring-georgia-special-election-runoff-a-big-r-win/\" target=\"_blank\">runoff election</a> in Georgia’s 6th Congressional District, several news outlets reported Thursday.</p>\n<!-- WP QUADS Content Ad Plugin v. 1.5.1 -->\n<div class=\"quads-location quads-ad1\" id=\"quads-ad1\" style=\"float:none;margin:3px 0 3px 0;text-align:center;\">\n<script async=\"\" src=\"//pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js\"></script>\n<!-- Political-article-top-336x280 -->\n<ins class=\"adsbygoogle\" style=\"display:inline-block;width:336px;height:280px\" data-ad-client=\"ca-pub-5711233193427660\" data-ad-slot=\"4660746438\" data-adsbygoogle-status=\"done\"><ins id=\"aswift_0_expand\" style=\"display:inline-table;border:none;height:280px;margin:0;padding:0;position:relative;visibility:visible;width:336px;background-color:transparent\"><ins id=\"aswift_0_anchor\" i=this.id,s=window.google_iframe_oncopy,H=s&amp;&amp;s.handlers,h=H&amp;&amp;H[i],w=this.contentWindow,d;try{d=w.document}catch(e){}if(h&amp;&amp;d&amp;&amp;(!d.body||!d.body.firstChild)){if(h.call){setTimeout(h,0)}else window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});\n</script>\n</div>\n\n<p>According to <a href=\"http://www.huffingtonpost.com/entry/georgia-voter-registration-runoff-ossoff_us_58f90c7ce4b06b9cb91505f8\" target=\"_blank\">The Huffington Post</a>, the Lawyers’ Committee for Civil Rights Under Law filed a complaint in the federal district court in Atlanta Thursday, arguing that the state is violating the National Voter Registration Act. That law sets 30 days before a federal election as the earliest permissible deadline for voter registration.</p>\n<p>Georgia complied with the provision for the special congressional election held this past Tuesday. But because no candidate won 50 percent of the vote, there will be a second election on June 20 ― a runoff between the top two finishers, Democrat Jon Ossoff and Republican Karen Handel.</p>\n<p>Georgia’s Secretary of State, a Republican, claims that the June runoff is simply a continuation of the special election this week, so election officials “don’t have to allow newly registered voters to participate.” The registration deadline for Tuesday’s election was March 20, and officials say anybody who registers after that day is not eligible to vote in the June runoff.</p>\n<p>Ezra Rosenberg, co-director of the voting rights project at the Lawyers’ Committee, argues that under the federal law, Georgia can’t set the registration deadline for the June 20 runoff any earlier than 30 days before that election ― that is, May 22, HuffPost states.</p>\n<p>“The case is actually a very, very simple case,” Rosenberg told reporters on a conference call Thursday. “Federal law specifically defines elections as including runoff elections.”</p>\n<p>The National Voter Registration Act, passed in 1993, defines the word “election” based on the Federal Election Campaign Act. That 1971 statute defines an election as “a general, special, primary,<strong> or runoff election.”</strong></p>\n<p>The lawsuit was filed on behalf of the Georgia NAACP, Georgia Coalition for the Peoples’ Agenda, ProGeorgia State Table, Third Sector Development and Asian Americans Advancing Justice-Atlanta. The groups are asking the federal court to order the state to let people vote on June 20 if they’re registered by May 22 ― and to publicize that extension of the deadline.</p>\n<p>Francys Johnson, president of the Georgia NAACP, called the decision to block people from voting “par for the course” for Georgia Secretary of State Brian Kemp (R). “The tactics that the secretary of state and the state of Georgia are employing are anything but special. They are typical,” Johnson told reporters.</p>\n<p>Their goal, Johnson argued, “is to make voting difficult, to make voting something that all Georgians cannot participate in. Any time there is a need to interpret federal law, [Kemp] always interprets federal law to close opportunities for Georgians to be able to exercise the right to vote.”</p>\n<p>Democratic challenger Jon Ossoff performed far stronger than expected in Tuesday’s election for the congressional seat recently vacated by Health and Human Services Secretary Tom Price. It’s a seat long held by Republicans.</p>\n<p>The race has drawn national attention because some see it as an early indicator that President Trump’s dwindling approval ratings could turn into political gains for Democrats.</p>\n<p>H/T: <a href=\"http://www.huffingtonpost.com/entry/georgia-voter-registration-runoff-ossoff_us_58f90c7ce4b06b9cb91505f8\" target=\"_blank\">Huffington Post.</a></p>\n\n<!-- WP QUADS Content Ad Plugin v. 1.5.1 -->\n<div class=\"quads-location quads-ad3\" id=\"quads-ad3\" style=\"float:none;margin:3px 0 3px 0;text-align:center;\">\n<script async=\"\"
